--- Commit Message ---
LU-18079 utils: argument parse opts for lfs quota

Adding new options to only get certain arguments from 'lfs quota'.
This works much like 'lfs getstripe'. Each option will show their
respected argument and can be combined together to show multiple
arguments. They will be shown in the same order that they appear
in the full table for 'lfs quota'.
Added:
    --filesystem|--mount-point
    --blocks|--space|--busage
    --block-softlimit|--bsoftlimit
    --block-hardlimit|--bhardlimit
    --block-grace|--bgrace|--btime
    --inodes|--iusage
    --inode-softlimit|--isoftlimit
    --inode-hardlimit|--ihardlimit
    --inode-grace|--igrace|--itime
each matching a column of the table.

--- Message (Etienne AUJAMES, 2024-10-09 10:05:27.000000000) ---
Patch Set 18: Code-Review+1

Hi,

I found this patch because some CEA's admins complain about parsing the "lfs quota" output. This patch is nice.

2 more things that would be great:
- An option to suppress the header line (--quiet or --no-header).
- An option to specify a custom char delimiter (--delimiter). We had some issues in the past with field displayed with an empty string (I think that was grace period for some cases, but I am not sure).

--- Message (Frederick Dilger, 2024-10-21 06:42:01.000000000) ---
Patch Set 18:

> Patch Set 18: Code-Review+1
> 
> Hi,
> 
> I found this patch because some CEA's admins complain about parsing the "lfs quota" output. This patch is nice.
> 
> 2 more things that would be great:
> - An option to suppress the header line (--quiet or --no-header).
> - An option to specify a custom char delimiter (--delimiter). We had some issues in the past with field displayed with an empty string (I think that was grace period for some cases, but I am not sure).

--quiet does in fact already exist and suppresses the header line, the delimiter option is a good idea, I'll put out a separate patch including that.
